*   [volta (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/ri7nz/zsh-volta) - Installs and loads [Volta: JS Toolchains as Code (‚≠ê11k)](https://github.com/volta-cli/volta).
*   [vscode (qianxinfeng) (‚≠ê33)](https://github.com/qianxinfeng/zsh-vscode) - Plugin for [Visual Studio Code](https://code.visualstudio.com/).
*   [wakatime (sobolevn) (‚≠ê91)](https://github.com/sobolevn/wakatime-zsh-plugin) - Track how much [time](https://wakatime.com/) you have spent in your terminal. Has per project stats.
*   [wakatime (wbingli) (‚≠ê152)](https://github.com/wbingli/zsh-wakatime) - Automatic time tracking for commands in ZSH using [wakatime](https://wakatime.com/).
*   [warhol (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/unixorn/warhol.plugin.zsh) - Configures colorization with [grc (‚≠ê1.9k)](https://github.com/garabik/grc).
*   [watch (‚≠ê17)](https://github.com/enrico9034/zsh-watch-plugin) - Easily prefix your current or previous commands with watch by pressing `CTRL + W`.
*   [watson.zsh (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/bcho/Watson.zsh) - A plugin for the [watson (‚≠ê2.5k)](https://github.com/TailorDev/Watson) time management system.
*   [wd (‚≠ê694)](https://github.com/mfaerevaag/wd) - Warp directory lets you jump to custom directories in ZSH, without using `cd`. Why? Because `cd` seems inefficient when the folder is frequently visited or has a long path.
*   [web-search (sinetoami) (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/sinetoami/web-search) - Add commands to run bing, google, yahoo, & duckduckgo searches directly from the CLI.
*   [web-search (yabanahano) (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/Yabanahano/web-search) - Adds aliases for searching with Google, Wiki, Bing, YouTube and other popular services.
*   [window-title (‚≠ê29)](https://github.com/olets/zsh-window-title) - Adds informative tiles to your terminal windows.
*   [windows-title (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/mdarocha/zsh-windows-title) - Dynamically updates terminal window title with current directory and the last command run.
*   [workon (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/bryanculver/workon.plugin.zsh) - Simple utility for jumping between projects.
*   [worktree (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/jspears/worktree) - Adds functions that wrap `git worktree`.
*   [xxh-plugin-zsh-zshrc (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/roman-geraskin/xxh-plugin-zsh-zshrc) - plugin for [xxh-shell-zsh (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/xxh/xxh-shell-zsh) that copies your `~/.zshrc` to a remote host and sources it with [xxh-shell-zsh (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/xxh/xxh-shell-zsh).
*   [you-should-use (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/MichaelAquilina/zsh-you-should-use) - ZSH plugin that reminds you to use those aliases you defined.
*   [youtube-dl-aliases (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/katrinleinweber/oh-my-zsh-youtube-dl-aliases) - Adds `yt` aliases to download videos from YouTube.
*   [youtube-dl (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/joow/youtube-dl) - Simple plugin for [youtube-dl](https://youtube-dl.org/).
*   [z.lua (‚≠ê3k)](https://github.com/skywind3000/z.lua) - A command line tool which helps you navigate faster by learning your habits. An alternative to [z.sh (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/rupa/z) with Windows and posix shells support and various improvements. 10x faster than fasd and autojump, 3x faster than [z.sh (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/rupa/z).
*   [zabb (‚≠ê39)](https://github.com/Mellbourn/zabb) - `zabb` is a command that tries to figure out the shortest memorable abbreviation of a directory that is usable by [z (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/ajeetdsouza/zoxide) to unambiguously jump to that directory.
*   [zabrze (‚≠ê34)](https://github.com/Ryooooooga/zabrze) - A ZSH abbreviation expansion plugin.
*   [zaw (‚≠ê576)](https://github.com/zsh-users/zaw) - ZSH anything.el-like widget.
*   [zce (‚≠ê60)](https://github.com/hchbaw/zce.zsh) - Vim's EasyMotion / Emacs's ace-jump-mode for ZSH.
*   [zcolors (‚≠ê80)](https://github.com/marlonrichert/zcolors) - Uses your `$LS_COLORS` to generate a coherent theme for Git and your Zsh prompt, completions and [ZSH syntax highlighting (‚≠ê20k)](https://github.com/zsh-users/zsh-syntax-highlighting).
*   [zconvey (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zconvey) - Adds ability to send commands to other ZSH sessions, you can use this to `cd $PWD` on all active ZSH sessions, for example.
*   [zed (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/eendroroy/zed-zsh) - A simple wrapper for [z (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/rupa/z) to install it via a ZSH plugin.
*   [zeno (‚≠ê166)](https://github.com/yuki-yano/zeno.zsh) - Fuzzy completion and utility plugin powered by [Deno](https://deno.land/).
*   [zero (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/arlimus/zero.zsh) - Zero is both a plugin and a theme. See the GitHub page for installation details. Includes `git` and `hg` status decorators.
*   [zflai (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zflai) - A fast logging framework for ZSH.
*   [zfzf (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/b0o/zfzf) - A fzf-powered file picker for ZSH which allows you to quickly navigate the directory hierarchy.
*   [zhooks (‚≠ê55)](https://github.com/agkozak/zhooks) - Displays the contents of any ZSH hook arrays and the code of any hook functions that have been defined. Useful for debugging.
*   [zinfo\_line (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/kmhjs/zinfo_line) - Makes more information available to ZSH themes.
*   [zinit-annex-bin-gem-node (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-bin-gem-node) - [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) extension that exposes binaries without altering `$PATH`, installs Ruby gems and Node modules and easily exposes their binaries, and updates the gems and modules when the associated plugin or snippet is updated.
*   [zinit-annex-default-ice (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-default-ice) - Allows user to define ices active for multiple zinit commands.
*   [zinit-annex-man (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-man) - [Zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) extension that generates man pages for all plugins and snippets
*   [zinit-annex-meta-plugins (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-meta-plugins) - Install groups of plugins with a single label ([zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) only).
*   [zinit-annex-patch-dl (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-patch-dl) - [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) extension that downloads files and applies patches through the provided `dl` and `patch` zinit ices.
*   [zinit-annex-readurl (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-readurl) - Adds function to automatically download the newest version of a file to which URL is hosted on a webpage.
*   [zinit-annex-rust (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-rust) - [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) extension that that installs rust and cargo packages inside plugin directories.
*   [zinit-annex-test (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/NorthIsMirror/z-a-test) - [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) extension that runs tests (via make test, for example) ‚Äì if it finds any of them ‚Äì after installing and updating a plugin or snippet.
*   [zinit-annex-unscope (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit-annex-unscope) - Allows installing plugins for [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) without specifying the user name by querying the Github API.
*   [zinit-console (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/z-shell/zinit-console) - A semigraphical (curses) consolette for the [zinit (‚≠ê3.1k)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit) plugin manager.
*   [zinsults (‚≠ê14)](https://github.com/ahmubashshir/zinsults) - Prints insults if a command fails.
*   [zjump (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/qoomon/zjump) - Simplify ZSH directory navigation; jump to already visited, parent or sub folders.
*   [zlitefetch (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/ippee/zlitefetch) - Lightweight system information plugin.
*   [zoxide (‚≠ê23k)](https://github.com/ajeetdsouza/zoxide) - A fast alternative to `cd` that learns your habits.
*   [zsh-select (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/z-shell/zsh-select) - Displays a selection list. It is similar to `selecta`, but uses the curses library to do display, and when compared to [fzf (‚≠ê65k)](https://github.com/junegunn/fzf), the main difference is approximate matching instead of fuzzy matching.
*   [zsh-z (agkozak) (‚≠ê2k)](https://github.com/agkozak/zsh-z) - Jump quickly to directories that you have visited "frecently." A native ZSH port of `z.sh` - without `awk`, `sed`, `sort`, or `date`.
*   [zsh-z (ptavares) (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/ptavares/zsh-z) - Installs and loads [z](https://github.com/rupa/z.git).
*   [zshrc (‚≠ê5)](https://github.com/freak2geek/zshrc) - Load local `.zshrc` files from your project scopes.
*   [zsnapac (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/johnramsden/zsh-zsnapac) - Plugin for taking ZFS pre/post upgrade snapshots on Arch Linux.
*   [zsnapshot (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zsnapshot) - Adds command to dump the current ZSH state into a file, for later restoration by sourcing the snapshot file.
*   [ztouch (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/mjrafferty/ztouch) - Adds touchbar controls for recent history commands, directory stack, cycling between modes and user-mappable commands to the touchbar on macOS.
*   [ztrace (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/ztrace) - Catches output of commands, allows to reuse that output, glue it with history content.
*   [zui (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zui) - ZSH User Interface library ‚Äì CGI+DHTML-like rapid TUI application development with ZSH.)

*   [pipenv (AlexGascon) (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/AlexGascon/pipenv-oh-my-zsh) - Enables aliases for the most common pipenv commands.
*   [pipenv (gangleri) (‚≠ê13)](https://github.com/gangleri/pipenv) - Completions for `pipenv`.
*   [pmy (‚≠ê142)](https://github.com/relastle/pmy) - General purpose context-aware ZSH completion engine powered by [fzf (‚≠ê65k)](https://github.com/junegunn/fzf).
*   [quickjump (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/fikovnik/zsh-quickjump) - Adds tab completion support for [skim (‚≠ê5.2k)](https://github.com/lotabout/skim) for recent files and directories using [fasd (‚≠ê76)](https://github.com/whjvenyl/fasd).
*   [racket completion (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/racket/shell-completion) - Completion for [Racket](http://racket-lang.org).
*   [rake-completion (‚≠ê8)](https://github.com/unixorn/rake-completion.zshplugin) - Add fast tab completion for rakefile targets.
*   [rhoas (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/craicoverflow/rhoas-zsh-plugin) - Adds completions for [rhoas](https://developers.redhat.com/products/red-hat-openshift-streams-for-apache-kafka/overview).
*   [rustup (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/pkulev/zsh-rustup-completion) - Tab completions for Rustup.
*   [s3cmd (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/FFKL/s3cmd-zsh-plugin) - Adds tab completions for [s3cmd](https://s3tools.org/s3cmd).
*   [salesforce-cli (‚≠ê90)](https://github.com/wadewegner/salesforce-cli-zsh-completion) - ZSH command completion for the Salesforce CLI. Requires [jq](https://stedolan.github.io/jq/).
*   [saml2aws (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/sirhc/saml2aws.plugin.zsh) - Adds completions for [saml2aws (‚≠ê2.1k)](https://github.com/Versent/saml2aws).
*   [spring-boot-plugin (‚≠ê10)](https://github.com/linux-china/oh-my-zsh-spring-boot-plugin) - Adds autocompletions for [spring-boot](http://projects.spring.io/spring-boot/) commands.
*   [ssh-agent (bobsoppe) (‚≠ê25)](https://github.com/bobsoppe/zsh-ssh-agent) - Manage `ssh-agent`.
*   [ssh-agent (hkupty) (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/hkupty/ssh-agent) - Automatically starts `ssh-agent` to set up and load whichever credentials you want for `ssh` connections.
*   [taskbook (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/mastern2k3/taskbook-zsh-plugin) - Auto-completes task numbers for taskbook.
*   [tmux pane words](https://gist.github.com/blueyed/6856354) - Key bindings to complete words from your [tmux](https://tmux.github.io) pane.
*   [tugboat (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/DimitriSteyaert/Zsh-tugboat) - Adds autocompletion for [tugboat (‚≠ê1.5k)](https://github.com/petems/tugboat) command.
*   [umake (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/zlsun/umake) - Tab completion for Ubuntu umake.
*   [vert.x (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/davidafsilva/vert.x-omz-plugin) - Provides autocomplete features for the [vertx](https://vertx.io/) command.
*   [web-open (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/AndrewHaluza/zsh-web-open) - Adds alias to open web pages. Only works with Ubuntu 20.
*   [yabai (‚≠ê16)](https://github.com/Amar1729/yabai-zsh-completions) - Add completions for macOS [yabai (‚≠ê24k)](https://github.com/koekeishiya/yabai/) tiling window manager.
*   [yarn (‚≠ê578)](https://github.com/g-plane/zsh-yarn-autocompletions) - Add autocompletions for `yarn add`, `yarn remove`, `yarn upgrade`, `yarn why` and `yarn run`.
*   [zargparse (‚≠ê12)](https://github.com/ctil/zargparse) - Pass it a script that uses `argparse` and it will write a ZSH completion to your current directory.

### Themes / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   [0i0 (‚≠ê15)](https://github.com/0i0/0i0.zsh-theme) - Optimized for dark terminal windows, uses nerdfont `git` status decorations.
*   [14degree (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/saims0n/14degree-zsh-theme/) - Includes `git`, `virtualenv` and `rvm` status decorations.
*   [1999 (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/DTan13/zsh1999) - Powerline-esque theme. Includes `git` status decorations, network and battery status.
*   [abbr (theme) (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/PhilsLab/abbr-zsh-theme) - Displays an abbreviated version of the current directory path, shows the Python virtualenv, Rust version, `git` status, and the exit code of last command. Works well on dark backgrounds by default but colors can be easily customized.
*   [adlee (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/adlee-was-taken/oh-my-zsh-osx/blob/master/adlee.zsh-theme) - macOS theme, requires a Powerline-compatible font.
*   [af-magic-dynamic (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/rslavin/af-magic-dynamic) - Modified version of [af-magic (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/andyfleming/oh-my-zsh/blob/master/themes/af-magic.zsh-theme) with dynamic path shortening.
*   [aflah-bhari (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/AflahB/aflah-bhari-zsh-theme) - Modified version of the [robbyrussell (‚≠ê174k)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/blob/master/themes/robbyrussell.zsh-theme) theme in oh-my-zsh.
*   [aftermath (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/schanur/aftermath) - Get a nice summary line after each command you run in your shell.
*   [agitnoster (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/dbestevez/agitnoster-theme) - Based on [agnoster](https://gist.github.com/3712874) theme included in [Oh My Zsh (‚≠ê174k)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh) and [bash-git-prompt (‚≠ê6.7k)](https://github.com/magicmonty/bash-git-prompt). Shows detailed information about `git` status.
*   [agkozak (‚≠ê292)](https://github.com/agkozak/agkozak-zsh-prompt) - Uses three asynchronous methods to keep the ZSH prompt responsive while displaying the `git` status and indicators of SSH connection, exit codes, and `vi` mode, along with an abbreviated, `PROMPT_DIRTRIM`-style path. Very customizable. Asynchronous even on Cygwin and MSYS2.
*   [agnoster-gentoo (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/r7l/agnoster-gentoo-zsh-theme) - A Gentoo flavored version of the [Agnoster ZSH Theme (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme) that includes user\@hostname and `git` status decorations. Works better with a unicode font.
*   [agnoster-mod (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/fsegouin/oh-my-zsh-agnoster-mod-theme) - [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) variant with a right-prompt.
*   [agnoster-plus (‚≠ê7)](https://github.com/jiahut/agnoster-plus.zsh-theme) - [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) variant optimized for use with [Solarized Dark (‚≠ê16k)](https://github.com/altercation/solarized/blob/master/iterm2-colors-solarized/Solarized%20Dark.itermcolors) terminal color scheme. Includes `git` status.
*   [agnoster-refresh (‚≠ê4)](https://github.com/fusion94/Agnoster-refresh) - [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) variant, includes battery and online status.
*   [agnoster-repopath (‚≠ê2)](https://github.com/ivanfurlan/agnoster-repopath-theme) - Based on [Agnoster (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme) and [Passion (‚≠ê301)](https://github.com/ChesterYue/ohmyzsh-theme-passion) themes. Includes `git` and `mercurial` status, current time and time the last command took decorations in the prompt.
*   [agnoster-timestamp-newline (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/DylanDelobel/agnoster-timestamp-newline-zsh-theme) - [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) variant with timestamp and newline added.
*   [agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) - Optimized for solarized terminal color schemes, shows `git` decorations, user\@host, working directory, the previous command's exit status and whether you are running with root privileges. Requires a Powerline-compatible font.
*   [agnosterAfro (‚≠ê6)](https://github.com/afrozalm/agnosterAfro) - Based on [Powerline (‚≠ê2.9k)](https://github.com/Lokaltog/vim-powerline) and [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874) themes and inspired by the [agnosterzak (‚≠ê388)](https://github.com/zakaziko99/agnosterzak-ohmyzsh-theme).
*   [agnosterzak (‚≠ê388)](https://github.com/zakaziko99/agnosterzak-ohmyzsh-theme) - Based on [Agnoster](https://gist.github.com/agnoster/3712874), shows battery life, date & time, `git` status, current directory and user & host information.
*   [akzsh (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/awkimball/akzsh) - Works best with a dark terminal theme, includes `git` decorations.
*   [alarangeiras (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/alarangeiras/alarangeiras-zsh-theme/) - Minimalist theme with `git` status decorations.
*   [ale (‚≠ê3)](https://github.com/alepimentel/ale-zsh) - Based on the fino theme. Includes `git`, `virtualenv` and `node` status decorations.
*   [alien-minimal (‚≠ê149)](https://github.com/eendroroy/alien-minimal) - Minimalist ZSH theme with `git` status displayed.
*   [alien (‚≠ê312)](https://github.com/eendroroy/alien) - Powerline-esque ZSH theme that shows `git` decorations and the exit code of the last command. Faster than many other prompts because it determines the `git` decorations asynchronously in a background process.
*   [almel (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/Ryooooooga/almel) - Inspired by [agnoster (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme), written in Rust. Includes `git` status, user\@host, last command exit status and working directory decorations
*   [alpharized (‚≠ê11)](https://github.com/NicoSantangelo/Alpharized) - Optimized to work with [solarized](http://ethanschoonover.com/solarized) dark terminals. It's a modified version of the [avit theme (‚≠ê174k)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh/blob/master/themes/avit.zsh-theme).

Inspired by [Agnoster (‚≠ê4k)](https://github.com/agnoster/agnoster-zsh-theme) and [Powerline (‚≠ê1.2k)](https://github.com/jeremyFreeAgent/oh-my-zsh-powerline-theme).

*   [prompt (‚≠ê0)](https://github.com/nathanblair/prompt) - A lightweight prompt consistent across `sh`, `dash`, `ash`, `zsh`, and `pwsh`. Includes `git` status decorations.

*   [pure (‚≠ê13k)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/pure) - A pretty, minimal and fast ZSH prompt. Includes `git` status decorations, prompt turns red if last command failed, username and host decorations when in a remote session or container, and current folder and command when a process is running.

It supports async segments using [zsh-async (‚≠ê769)](https://github.com/mafredri/zsh-async).

*   [zshred (‚≠ê1)](https://github.com/redxtech/zshred) - Shows current directory, `git` decorations, exit status of last command and time.

### ZSH Tools / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   [zsh-bench (‚≠ê626)](https://github.com/romkatv/zsh-bench) - A benchmark for interactive ZSH. It measures user-visible latency of interactive `zsh`: input lag, command lag, etc.
*   [zshdb (‚≠ê295)](https://github.com/rocky/zshdb) - A ZSH debugger.
*   [zshelldoc (‚≠ê18)](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zshelldoc) - Doxygen for shell scripts. Parses ZSH and Bash scripts, outputs Asciidoc document with function lists, call trees, lists of exported variables, and more.
*   [zunit (‚≠ê208)](https://github.com/zunit-zsh/zunit) - A powerful unit testing framework for ZSH.

### Other Useful Lists / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   [awesome-devenv (‚≠ê2.8k)](https://github.com/jondot/awesome-devenv) - A curated list of awesome tools, resources and workflow tips making an awesome development environment.
*   [awesome-sysadmin (‚≠ê25k)](https://github.com/n1trux/awesome-sysadmin) - A curated list of awesome open source sysadmin resources.
*   [Terminals Are Sexy (‚≠ê12k)](https://github.com/k4m4/terminals-are-sexy) - A curated list for CLI lovers.

## [Oct 30, 2021](/content/2021/10/30/README.md)

### [Zinit](https://github.com/zdharma-continuum/zinit)

*   Turbo mode ‚Äì 80% faster ZSH startup! for example: instead of 200 ms, it'll be 40 ms
*   Completion management (selectively disable and enable completions)
*   Snippets (‚Üî regular files downloaded via-URL, e.g.: scripts) and through them Oh My Zsh and Prezto plugins support (‚Üí low overhead)
*   Annexes (‚Üî Zinit extensions)
*   Reports (from the plugin loads ‚Äì plugins are no longer black boxes)
*   Plugin unloading (allows e.g.: dynamic theme switching)
*   `bindkey` capturing and remapping
*   packages
*   Clean `fpath` (the array `$fpath` is not being used to add completions and autoload functions, hence it stays concise, not bloated)
*   Services ‚Üî a single-instance, background plugins
*   Also, in general: all the mechanisms from the ZSH Plugin Standard ‚Äì Zinit is a reference implementation of the standard.

## [Feb 03, 2021](/content/2021/02/03/README.md)

### [znap](https://github.com/marlonrichert/zsh-snap)

*   Multi-repo management
*   Automatic `compinit` and `bashinit` - you no longer need them in your `.zshrc`, znap will do them automatically as needed.

## [Sep 22, 2020](/content/2020/09/22/README.md)

### [znap](https://github.com/marlonrichert/zsh-snap)

*   Make any prompt appear instantly. Reduce your startup time from \~200ms to \~40ms with just one command.
*   Asynchronously compile your plugins and functions.
*   Cache those expensive `eval $(commands)`.
*   Clone or pull multiple repos in parallel.
*   Re-clone all your repos without you having to re-enter them.

## [Sep 03, 2020](/content/2020/09/03/README.md)

### zinit

*   1 line install

## [Sep 01, 2018](/content/2018/09/01/README.md)

### [zplug](https://github.com/zplug/zplug)

*   Can manage everything
    *   ZSH plugins/UNIX commands on [GitHub](https://github.com) and [Bitbucket](https://bitbucket.org)
    *   Gist files ([gist.github.com](https://gist.github.com/discover))
    *   Externally managed plugins e.g., [oh-my-zsh (‚≠ê174k)](https://github.com/ohmyzsh/ohmyzsh) and [prezto (‚≠ê14k)](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto) plugins/themes
    *   Binary artifacts on [GitHub Releases](https://help.github.com/articles/about-releases/)
    *   Local plugins
    *   etc. (you can add your [own sources (‚≠ê5.8k)](https://github.com/zplug/zplug/blob/master/doc/guide/External-Sources.md)!)
*   Super-fast parallel installation/update
*   Support for lazy-loading
*   Branch/tag/commit support
*   Post-update, post-load hooks
*   Interactive interface ([fzf (‚≠ê65k)](https://github.com/junegunn/fzf), [peco (‚≠ê7.7k)](https://github.com/peco/peco), [zaw (‚≠ê576)](https://github.com/zsh-users/zaw), and so on)
*   Cache mechanism for reducing [the startup time (‚≠ê5.8k)](https://github.com/zplug/zplug#vs)

## [Oct 07, 2014](/content/2014/10/07/README.md)

### [dotzsh](https://github.com/dotphiles/dotzsh) / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   Load the plugin module in `.zshrc`

### [Oh-My-Zsh](http://ohmyz.sh/) / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   `cd ~/.oh-my-zsh/custom/plugins`
*   `git clone repo`

### [Prezto](https://github.com/sorin-ionescu/prezto) / [superconsole](https://github.com/alexchmykhalo/superconsole) - Windows-only

*   Clone the plugin into your prezto modules directory
*   Add the plugin to your `.zpreztorc` file
*   Open a new terminal window or tab
